Initial Results of the French General Election 88

Show a Leftward Trend

Socialist and Radical Parties Unite

The Current Cabinet Is in Danger of Collapse

National News Agency, Paris, 2nd - The current French election clearly shows a trend towards the left. The Tardieu cabinet is therefore in danger, and former Prime Minister Herriot, the leader of the Radical Socialist Party, may be able to form a cabinet. Now, with the union of the Socialist Party and the Radical Socialist Party, the Tardieu cabinet is in even greater danger. Today, Herriot and Frossard issued separate statements declaring that in the second round of voting next Sunday, in districts where the Radical Socialist Party received the most votes in the first round, Socialist Party voters should vote for the Radical Socialist Party candidate. Conversely, in districts where the Socialist Party received the most votes, Radical Socialist Party voters should also vote for the Socialist Party candidate. Previously, the two parties had expressed unwillingness to share responsibility in a joint coalition cabinet, but the sudden move to coordinate elections has greatly surprised observers. According to the latest reports, 244 members of parliament were elected in the first round of voting yesterday, and 359 more will be elected in the second round. Among those elected in the first round, the current government faction won only 115 seats, while the opposition won 129 seats. The number of voters was about 80 percent. Havas, Paris, 2nd - The results of the first round of the French general election for the Chamber of Deputies yesterday are as follows: Conservative Party 3 seats, Republican Party 72 seats, Left Republican Party 32 seats. These three parties are collectively known as the Right Wing, with a total of 107 seats. Radical Republican Party 24 seats, Radical Socialist Party 60 seats, Republican Socialist Party 17 seats, Socialist Party 41 seats. These four parties are collectively known as the Left Wing, with a total of 142 seats. Communist Party 2 seats. A total of 615 members of parliament should be elected to the Chamber of Deputies this time. In addition to those already elected, there are 364 remaining, who did not receive the required number of votes and must be decided in the second round of voting next Sunday. Based on the results already confirmed, the Conservative Party lost one seat compared to the previous election, the Republican Party gained two new seats, the Left Republican Party lost eight seats, the Radical Republican Party gained four more seats, and the Socialist Party gained one more seat. The Communist Party's position remained unchanged. All current cabinet members, including Prime Minister Tardieu, were elected in the first round. The leaders of the parties that stood in opposition to Tardieu in the current parliament (such as the Socialist Party, the Radical Socialist Party, and the Communist Party), such as Léon Blum, Herriot, and Frossard, have all been elected.

Reuters, Paris, 1st - Although the final results of the French general election are not yet known, the important leaders of each party were easily elected. Prime Minister Tardieu has been elected, with 3,000 more votes than his opponent, and Justice Minister Raynaud, Tardieu's great assistant, was also elected in the Paris constituency. The well-known Radical Party leader Herriot was also elected in Lyon. Saigon's results arrived earlier due to time constraints, but no one was elected in Saigon, so a second round of voting is necessary. Former Prime Minister Painlevé, Minister of Commerce Rollin, Socialist Party leader Blum, and Chamber Speaker Marin were all re-elected. However, Socialist Party Secretary-General Sarrat was defeated. Many people were stationed outside newspaper offices today waiting for the election results.

National News Agency, Paris, 1st - According to preliminary reports released tonight, the Radical Socialist Party's strength has greatly increased in today's general election due to public dissatisfaction with the current government's policies. Although the final results will not be confirmed until after the second round of voting next Sunday, today's first round of voting clearly indicates that the number of Radical Socialist Party seats will greatly increase compared to before. Conversely, the Socialist Party can only maintain its original position. Radical Socialist Party leader Herriot was elected in the first round of voting, with more than 2,500 more votes than each candidate. Former party chairman Daladier and other prominent politicians such as Reynaud, Lièche, Rollin, and the blind parliamentarian Sabatier were also elected. Although the country was under strict military and police surveillance today, many conflicts still occurred. Even in Tardieu's constituency of Belfort, there were clashes between Radical Socialist Party members and right-wing party members. However, the capital was relatively peaceful, with only small conflicts between the Young Patriots and the Communist Party. The group rushed into the Ivry town hall, clashed with the Communist guards, and then removed the red flag and hung the tricolor flag, because its city council was controlled by the Communist Party, so the town hall flew the red flag.

Inukai's Broadcast Speech 90

Claims Peace While Forcing Military Aggression

British Conservative Party Members Confused by Japanese Propaganda

Dentsu, Tokyo, 2nd - Prime Minister Inukai gave a radio broadcast speech from his official residence at 7:00 PM last night, titled "Countermeasures for Domestic and Foreign Troubles," as yesterday was Labor Day. Regarding the China issue, he said: "Currently, various disputes have occurred with neighboring countries. This situation is not only unfortunate for each other, but also unfortunate for the world. There are three reasons for this. First, red elements are trying to incite international disputes. Second, there are those who make it their job to boycott Japanese goods. Third, some incite anti-Japanese sentiment due to internal affairs. Although there are various reasons, the fundamental reason lies in unequal treaties. As for extraterritoriality, we had quite a bit of experience in the abolition movement when we were young, so we deeply sympathize with China. Japan sincerely hopes to find a way to befriend China from the root, so it also hopes that China will make efforts like Japan did in the past to complete its legal code and first establish parliamentary and constitutional politics to break the current one-party dictatorship and seek national unity. This is a prerequisite. Some countries misunderstand Japan as being aggressive, but the Seiyukai's industrialization policy proves that the Japanese people love peace. The Manchurian Incident was a last resort, resorting to force was not initiated by Japan. On this point, one should not simply accuse us of aggression. I hope they will fully recognize and awaken to this." Reuters, London, 30th - Conservative Party Member of Parliament Major-General Knocks praised Foreign Minister Simon's calm and alert attitude in Geneva regarding the Sino-Japanese conflict in a speech to Conservative Party members in Slough today. He said that the British people should all be grateful for his efforts to maintain peace. He also said that since the Japanese army is now fighting against communist forces, Britain must treat Japan, which is performing brave work for the British as a fellow country, fairly.

British Scientists Successfully Test Atomic Fission 91

Breaking the Theory of Atomic Permanence

Reuters, London, 2nd - A report says that British Cambridge scientists Dr. Cockcroft and Dr. Walton have invented a method to split atoms. According to Dr. Cockcroft, he tested with light hydrogen atoms, using about 120,000 volts of electricity, which was enough to split the atom into helium. The two doctors have been testing for many years under the guidance of Lord Rutherford. Lord Rutherford said that the doctor's invention is difficult to use commercially at present, but it is extremely important scientifically. According to atomic theory, all matter is made up of several kinds of extremely small atoms. Those belonging to the same kind have the same size, weight, and other properties. Since the invention of modern radioactivity, the theory of atomic permanence and indivisibility has gradually been shaken. Helium is the lightest gas and is very much needed on airships.

The most severe area was the Marseille region, where residents fled their homes in their sleep. Near the town of Billy-Ville, a farmhouse collapsed, killing three people. Japan Splits into Soft and Hard Factions on League of Nations Resolution 93

The Hardliners are Willing to Sever Relations with the League of Nations

The Compromisers Advocate Avoiding Head-on Confrontation

The Osaka Asahi Shimbun said that, with the resolution of the Continued Committee as the center, two major compromise proposals were put forward to ease the profound confrontation between Japan and the League of Nations: (1) the proposal of British Minister to China Lampson, and (2) the proposal of League of Nations Deputy Secretary-General Sugimura Yotaro. The contents of the two proposals are extremely confidential within the government. Generally speaking, the final withdrawal time of the Japanese army and the authority of the League of Nations Committee will be revised in the resolution to determine a compromise point between Japan and the League of Nations' opposing claims. However, in this situation, the government suddenly saw the emergence of the opposing views of compromise and non-compromise factions. The hardliners did not recognize the Continued Committee and rejected all actions of the Continued Committee interfering with the Shanghai truce negotiations, and resolutely did not allow withdrawal or change according to the established policy. If the League of Nations does not reflect on its current attitude, Japan will have no choice but to sever relations with the League of Nations. The softliners advocated avoiding a head-on confrontation with the League of Nations and resolving the situation with a policy of political compromise. That is, the decision on the final withdrawal time of the Japanese army cannot be carried out according to the authority of the committee, but the committee can submit its opinions on the situation in Shanghai to the League of Nations, so as to leave room for compromise. As a result of the division of opinions between the two factions, it was impossible to decide on a foreign policy. However, Foreign Minister Yoshizawa was very sympathetic to the compromisers, believing that political compromise could avoid conflict with the League of Nations. (Translator's note: The non-compromise faction is the minority militarist faction, who despise the League of Nations and believe that force can subdue justice, while the literati faction understands the trends of international affairs and dares not act arbitrarily, simply inviting the world's jealousy, so they are willing to give in and strive for a solution.)

Soviet Russia Prepares the Whole Country to Participate in National Defense 94

All Sectors of the Country Are Mobilized Uniformly

Twelve Million Pilots

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun's Moscow dispatch states that the total number of Communist Party members in Soviet Russia this year who are of conscription age has reached millions. According to the announcement by the Soviet Russian authorities, physical examinations will be carried out for people of eligible age to prepare them to participate in national defense in times of emergency, and work will be assigned to them during national defense wars. On the other hand, a wartime system has also been announced for the 12 million members of the International Cultural Aviation Association, forcing all members to engage in military training. At the same time, an order has been issued to all schools and factories in Russia to enforce military training. Therefore, in fact, except for farmers and a small number of special classes, all Russian citizens are prepared to participate in national defense.

Shanghai Citizens' Federation Initiates Memorial Service for Fallen Anti-Japanese Soldiers 97

Yesterday's Letter to Various Organizations Requests Representatives to Attend

The Shanghai Citizens' Federation, in view of the considerable number of loyal and brave soldiers who sacrificed themselves to defend the nation against Japan since the beginning of the Shanghai War, as well as innocent civilians who were brutally murdered by the violent Japanese, has initiated a memorial service for the fallen anti-Japanese soldiers and victimized compatriots. Yesterday, letters were sent to various organizations and native-place associations, requesting them to send representatives to participate. The original letter stated: "To whom it may concern: Since the January 28th Shanghai War, our loyal 19th Route Army and 5th Army soldiers have united to resist foreign aggression for the sake of national survival, fighting fiercely for over thirty days, finally causing the stubborn and violent Japanese to restrain their ferocity and fail in their designs. Their arduous and outstanding battle achievements have shocked the world. However, since the war, many of our loyal and brave frontline soldiers have also sacrificed themselves in righteous causes. The aspirations and spirit of these martyrs who achieved benevolence and took righteousness will forever remain in the heavens and earth. Furthermore, in this Songhu war zone, countless compatriots have suffered casualties from bullets and shells and have been innocently massacred by the Japanese invaders. Alas, how can our compatriots rest in peace? Overcome with grief, our association has initiated a preparatory office for the memorial service for the fallen anti-Japanese soldiers and victimized compatriots, located at No. 21 Hongxiang Lane, Xinzha Road. We now specially seek participation from all sectors, organizations, and native-place associations. Those who wish to participate are requested to nominate representatives to jointly initiate the event. Please reply within five days of receiving this letter so that we can notify you to attend the meeting. Your attention and cooperation are greatly appreciated."

The newly appointed Superintendent of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, Mr. Chen Fumu, arrived at the company yesterday at 9:00 AM during the weekly memorial service to assume his duties. Due to the numerous affairs of the Ministry, I was delayed until today to assume my duties. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is the largest shipping organization in our country, with excellent docks and huge warehouses. Now, I hope that everyone will completely eradicate all previous bad habits and become a perfect China Merchants Steam Navigation Company employee. Although I was appointed by the government, I am not here to be an official, but to serve. I have always had no concept of class. Most of you are colleagues. Section chiefs and secretaries are distinctions of position, but everyone has the same rights in doing things, and there is no hierarchy. Regarding areas of the company that need reform, anyone with good plans can submit them for consideration. However, you must consider the overall situation and not just your personal interests. If you think that the reform measures of the Superintendent's office are not appropriate, you can also state your opinions. As long as it is beneficial to the company and unrelated to personal matters, it will be accepted." After Mr. Chen's speech, he was accompanied by Mr. Li back to the Superintendent's office on the third floor to briefly handle the affairs of the Superintendent. Due to the numerous affairs of the Ministry, he returned to Nanjing in the afternoon. According to Mr. Chen, the swearing-in ceremony may not be necessary.

Minimum Electricity Charge and Meter Deposits 100

Shanghai Power Company Prepares to Eliminate Extra Collections

Shanghai Power Company announces: "The practice of electricity supply companies charging a minimum electricity fee to users is a common practice worldwide. This method is sometimes directly collected under the name of a minimum electricity fee, and sometimes collected under the name of meter rental. Currently, Shanghai Power Company adopts the former method. The direct collection of a minimum electricity fee is most suitable for situations where a user's electricity bill is less than a certain limit, and is fairer than collecting meter rental. Since a user requests electricity supply from the company but does not use it, the electricity supply company must charge a minimum electricity fee, partly to compensate for the company's interest on capital invested in electricity supply, and partly to subsidize the costs of meter reading and accounting. If a meter rental system is adopted, this rental must be included in the electricity bill and collected together, regardless of the amount of electricity used, which loses the meaning of a minimum electricity fee. Shanghai Power Company does not adopt meter rental, but adopts a minimum electricity fee restriction, precisely because this restriction is extremely fair and does not increase the burden on general users who have already used electricity supply. The origin of the minimum electricity fee is actually due to the necessity for electricity supply companies to also have protection. Electricity supply companies often find that the amount of electricity used by users is so small that the actual electricity bill is not commensurate with the expenses incurred for electricity supply. Therefore, companies need a certain degree of protection in terms of electricity supply. The minimum electricity fee is the result of this necessary protection. The purpose of adopting a minimum electricity fee is by no means to make a profit, but to provide a kind of protection against unreasonable losses. In fact, situations where a minimum electricity fee applies are rare. However, the company has set this restriction to avoid uncompensated expenses, which is fair and necessary as mentioned above. The minimum electricity fee adopted by Shanghai Power Company, before the change to monthly billing, was 3.75 taels. Now that the billing has been changed to monthly, this minimum electricity fee has been reduced to one-third, totaling 1.25 taels. Here are examples to illustrate the amount of the 70% minimum electricity fee. Assuming that a user has three 50-candlepower electric lamps and uses them for an average of three hours per day in a month, the electricity bill for a month, calculated at the current tariff, should be 1.6 taels of silver, which already exceeds the minimum electricity fee stipulated by our company. As for collecting meter deposits for electricity supply, this is also a common practice nowadays. A little observation of the situation can show that it is very fair. Electricity matters are very different from other types of businesses. After one party supplies electricity and the other party uses it, a long time must pass before an account can be opened and payment collected. In general, in Shanghai, from the time a user starts using electricity, they begin to owe the company electricity fees until the day of payment, which is about two months. That is, the user has received and used electricity for two months before paying the electricity bill. This fact is very unfavorable to the company, because under these circumstances, the company has to bear the loss of monthly interest on electricity supply expenses, and at the same time, there is a risk of users defaulting on electricity bills. This default can occur at any time. Therefore, electricity supply requires users to pay a cash deposit to cover the cost of two months of electricity usage. In Shanghai, this has become a long-standing practice. Our company has recently adopted a new accounting system and changed the old practice of collecting user electricity bills every three months to collecting them monthly. Because of this reform, our company believes that the amount of user deposits should also be reduced accordingly. We have already started to handle this, namely, reducing the amount of newly collected deposits and also refunding existing deposits where there is a clear overpayment according to the current method. However, the company's management of electricity fee deposits must be based on each user's monthly electricity usage to determine the amount to be refunded. Currently, there are as many as 65,000 users whose accounts need to be adjusted. With so many users, the adjustment is extremely cumbersome and cannot be completed in a short time. We must declare this to all sectors and ask for their understanding. Our company has absolutely no intention of withholding deposits that exceed reasonable business guarantees. Our company has already started and will continue to work hard to complete the deposit adjustment within a reasonable period. We hope that all sectors will thoroughly understand this as well. Shanghai Power Company announces."

Record of the Meeting of the Shanghai Pudong District Rent Reduction Association 101

The Pudong District Rent Reduction Movement Committee held a meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday at the second floor of No. 20 Museum Road. Representatives from Huishan Road, Dalian Bay Road, Huade Road, Qiqihar Road, Taopeng Road, Zhoushan Road, Yulin Road, Linqing Road, Yangzhou Road, Songpan Road, Longjiang Road, Bekaier Road, Pingliang Road, Zhoujiazui Road, Jinsheng Road, Haizhou Road, Liaoyang Road, Ningguo Road, Qiwupu Road, Danyang Road, and Jingzhou Road, as well as You Jingqing, Li Deliang, Guo Shifu, Shan Xingwu, Gu Rui, Liu Chunsheng, Zhao Guiting, Wu Baosheng, Sun Shumo, Zhou Bingheng, Qiu Wenbing, and others, totaling over one hundred people, attended. You Jingqing was elected as chairman and Gu Rui as secretary. The chairman reported that since the Shanghai War, Pudong has faced the Huangpu River, backed onto Jiangwan, with the Japanese headquarters on the left and the Japanese landing site on the right. Security is tight, and the situation is special. To this day, various roads are still in a state of terror, with military vehicles constantly transporting supplies, military telephones still being installed, and barracks everywhere. Most of our residents, both men and women, are laborers. Although they have managed to avoid the worst for the time being, they are ultimately unable to relocate far away. Their unsettled living conditions are known to all. Moreover, the livelihood of unemployed workers is currently dependent on the relief efforts of society. How can they afford to pay rent? Our residents are not only burdened by their usual economic difficulties but also affected by the war. To seek adjustment, there is no other way than to reduce or exempt rent. Recently, enthusiastic individuals from the Citizens' Federation and other groups have initiated movements, but the Pudong area is vast. Without a strict organizational foundation, it is insufficient to provide support. Therefore, the labor unions of various factories and the residents of various industries have jointly organized this association, which is why it has emerged. How to proceed from now on? I hope that all representatives will share their great opinions and work together to achieve final victory. The resolutions of the meeting are recorded below: (1) A motion to ratify the association's previous nomination of You Jingqing, Guo Shifu, and Liu Chunsheng as representatives to attend the Citizens' Federation's district representatives' meeting was passed. (2) A motion on whether the association should join the Citizens' Federation's united movement was passed. (3) A motion on how to reduce or exempt rent in the district was resolved to be handled in accordance with the resolutions of the Citizens' Federation's district representatives' meeting. (4) A motion on how to elect the association's committee members was resolved that, in addition to the initiators being ex officio members, Xu Duo, Luo Jizhuang, Dong Juanying, Wang Lifu, Zhu Haidong, Bao Ziheng, Jiang Zhengping, Zhu Qingyu, and Shen Jinkui be additionally appointed as committee members. (5) A motion on how to collect statistics on residents in the district was resolved that representatives from each district should separately notify and register with the association. (6) A motion on how to raise funds for the association was resolved that each labor union and committee member should bear the costs equally, without collecting membership fees. (7) A motion on whether to hire legal counsel for the association was resolved to hire lawyers Wu Chengyu, Liu Hong, and Wang Peiyuan as legal counsel for the association and to publish it in the newspaper. (8) The meeting was adjourned.

Red Cross Songjiang Wounded Soldier Hospital Closes 103

The Shanghai General Office of the Chinese Red Cross, considering that Songjiang, located on the Shanghai-Hangzhou route and close to the war zone, was in urgent need of relief efforts due to the Japanese occupation of the Shanghai waterfront, requested the Chairman of the Songjiang Branch, Mr. Zhou Jun Xuewen, to convene leaders from all sectors to establish the 43rd Wounded Soldier Hospital. Since its establishment two months ago, it has now announced its closure. Its announcement states: "During the recent Shanghai War, Songjiang City was in close proximity. Our branch was ordered by the General Office to establish the 43rd Wounded Soldier Hospital at the Songjiang Malu Bridge Bus Station to provide relief to wounded and sick soldiers, which is our duty and cannot be shirked. The necessary medical supplies, clothing, and other expenses were all approved and provided by the General Office, and no donations were solicited locally. With the situation easing, it has been decided to close the hospital on the 30th of this month, settle all public accounts, and if there are any omissions or payments that have not been processed, please invite the original handlers to the hospital within five days to verify and collect them to complete the procedures. No claims will be recognized after the deadline. This is a solemn announcement. The Red Cross's cause is purely a charitable and voluntary undertaking, which is readily supported by people at home and abroad. However, it is feared that there may be cases of people deceiving others under false pretenses, which cannot be avoided. The hospital director, in view of this, is afraid of causing problems and has to make a strict statement."

Chen Zhixin Discards His Sister and Defiles Her Sister 104

Sister Accuses Chen of Abandonment

Requests a Large Sum for Living Expenses

Chen Zhixin, also known as Zhongying and Zheng Zhenping, 34 years old, a local and owner of the Changlun Paper Store at No. 44 Yongan Street, French Concession, married Qian Yuezhu from Suzhou (now 21 years old, formerly a prostitute under the name Bao Ruiyun No. 5 in the Xiaohuayuan) as a concubine in 1930. However, not long after, Chen became infatuated with Yuezhu's older sister and discarded Yuezhu like worn-out shoes. Therefore, Yuezhu hired lawyer Jiang Qishi to file a lawsuit with the Second Special Court, accusing Chen of abandonment. The lawsuit reads as follows: "He loved me at first but abandoned me in the end, ignoring my illness and hunger. Please investigate to uphold the law and protect my life. I was born into a poor family and once worked in a brothel. The defendant often came to visit and we became acquainted. At that time, he was extremely affectionate towards me, and I admired Chen because of his good family background. So, we fell in love, and in February 1930, we agreed that he would pay 3,500 yuan to my adoptive mother, Jiang, to redeem me and take me as a concubine, with a monthly expense of 100 yuan. On November 28 of the same year, I gave birth to a daughter, named Xiajuan, who is now three years old. Until July of last year, my older sister came to visit. Chen saw that my sister was beautiful and became infatuated with her, and gradually became disgusted with me. He relapsed and used his seductive tricks. My sister fell into his trap, and they found a house to live together. When I found out and confronted him, Chen used sweet words and all kinds of deceptions to trick me. He even asked his friend, Mr. Liu Chaokui, to persuade me to live with his first wife and promised to break up with my sister. I believed him and moved into the old house where his legal wife lived. But in less than two months, I learned that Chen and my sister were still living together in Wenyuanfang. His behavior towards me completely changed. The lovers of the past became enemies. Occasionally when he came home, a disagreement would lead to loud insults and scolding. If he was not satisfied, he would resort to physical abuse. His wife was by his side, assisting the evildoer, intending to force me to leave. Unable to bear the abuse, I had no choice but to return to my mother's house temporarily in January of this year to avoid further abuse. On the one hand, I entrusted a lawyer to send a letter requesting living expenses, but it has been three months and he has ignored it, abandoning me like worn-out shoes. Although I am illiterate, I know a little about etiquette. A woman should follow her husband until the end. Now I am poor and helpless, unable to remarry, and have no means of making a living. The defendant, Chen Zhixin, is wealthy, with assets of more than 300,000 yuan. It is no problem for him to support me. His heart is so cruel, which is beyond my expectations and shocks all my relatives and friends. I have nowhere to go, and I am suffering from poverty and illness. If this continues, my remaining life will be hard to save. I, his wife, have been forced to beg, with tears in my eyes, that he be punished for abandonment under Article 310 of the Criminal Law and ordered to pay 48,000 yuan in living expenses in one lump sum so that it can be deposited in a money house to live off the interest, and that I be allowed to adopt my young daughter and that he be ordered to pay for her upbringing and dowry expenses, and that he return my jewelry, clothes, household furniture, etc." Yesterday, Chen did not appear when summoned. The court ordered that he be summoned again for investigation.

The night before, Xu Youxi, from Gaoyou, gathered a group of people to steal rice from the Luniklai rice ship at the wharf. Zhang Yuquan saw this and stepped forward to stop them. Xu, relying on his superior numbers, made trouble for Zhang. In desperation, Zhang grabbed a sharp knife, grabbed Xu, and stabbed him wildly, causing fatal injuries and instant death. Wang Wei, Xu's relative, reported the incident to the Third District Second Precinct, which dispatched police to arrest the two Zhangs and Gao. As the case involved a death, they were all transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

A Cry for Help in the Middle of the Night 107

Security Guard Fires a Shot

One Thief Escapes, One is Captured

Woman and Pigeons Rescued

Around 1:00 AM the night before, a cry for help was suddenly heard in the Xiaowujiazhai area southwest of the Qichang Wharf in Pudong. Security guards from the Yangjing District Protection Corps, who were patrolling nearby, went to investigate. In the darkness, they saw two men dragging a woman out of a bamboo fence and walking towards the wheat field. The guards suspected they were bandits and fired a shot, ordering them to stop. One man immediately fell to the ground, while the other ran away. They abandoned a cloth bag (containing five white pigeons). The injured man and the woman, along with the pigeons, were taken to the corps headquarters. That night, after questioning by Corps Commander Xu, the woman stated that her name was Zhuang Chen, from Pudong, living at No. 4 Xiaowujiazhai. Her husband's name was Zhuang Fugui, a farmer. Tonight, she heard the dogs barking loudly. When she opened the door to investigate, she saw that the bamboo door was open, and there were shadows in front of the house. She shouted "Thief!" Suddenly, two men rushed out and dragged her to the field, so she shouted for help. Fortunately, the Protection Corps came to her rescue and captured one man. The five pigeons were raised by my family and were stolen by them and dropped on the road. The injured man stated that his name was Wang Yongsheng, from Zhenjiang, 43 years old. He had come to Shanghai a few days ago to find his brother but had not found him. He was staying in a hostel in Xiaodongmen. Tonight, he was persuaded by Wang Mazi, who was outside, to come to Pudong. He did not know that Wang was stealing things, which led to his capture. Wang's left sole was found to have been pierced by a bullet, but it was not a serious injury. The suspects and witnesses were sent to the Third District, then transferred to the Public Security Bureau for disposal yesterday.

Public Concession Deputy Commissioner of Police, Aier S, Takes Leave to Return Home 110

Will Return to His Original Position After Seven Months of Leave

Aier S, the British Chief Inspector and Deputy Commissioner of Police of the Public Concession, has served in the police department in Shanghai since 1900, a total of 32 years, making him the longest-serving police officer in Shanghai. He is known for his integrity and impartiality, and is deeply respected by both Chinese and foreigners. He is currently 50 years old and in good spirits. Having lived in Shanghai for many years, he is eager to return to his hometown and has been granted leave. He is scheduled to depart for home today for a period of seven months. The Bankers' Association, the Industry Association, the Exchange Association, and leaders from various industries have all presented him with commendations and prepared to send representatives to the dock to see him off. It is said that Mr. Aier S will return to his original position after his leave.

Kidnapper Zhang Jiarong Executed by Firing Squad 111

Zhang's Attitude Was Very Tough

Said He Had Nothing Else to Say Since Death Was Imminent

Kidnapper Zhang Jiarong, a native of Jiangbei, 25 years old, was found to have conspired with others to kidnap four-month-old Yuan Genbao at gunpoint on April 5, 1928, at No. 1332 Yangshupu Road, extorting a large sum of money and robbing the Jufeng Pawnshop on the same road before escaping. After the case was reported, he was arrested by Chief Detective Wang Chengying of the General Patrol Station and sent to the Special District Local Court for trial, where he was sentenced to death. After the sentence was approved by the higher authorities, he was ordered to be executed. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang Hechun of the Fifth Criminal Court arrived and ordered the police to bring Zhang to the court and asked if he had any last words and sent a letter to his family. Zhang Jiarong's attitude was tough and unafraid, stating, "My name is also Xiao Zhang. Today, death is imminent, and I have nothing else to say. I don't need to communicate with my parents. In short, I am unfilial." His eyes glared at the patrol station detectives, and he spoke disrespectfully, saying, "Quickly send me to Caoh Jing for execution." The court ordered the Chinese and Western police to take him away. Zhang raised his hands and asked the Western police to handcuff him, exclaiming, "I'm going to heaven!" The Chinese and Western police then escorted him onto a car, along with the case files and photographs, and drove to the execution ground at the Second Prison in Caoh Jing. The execution officer appointed by the Local Court arrived at the scene, confirmed the identity of Zhang as the person named, and ordered the bailiffs to tie him up according to the law and execute him by firing squad.

Methods for Reprinting Anti-Japanese Western Propaganda Materials 113

The Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the League of Nations Investigation Team, along with a lengthy article. Based on materials from Westerners and Japanese, it refutes various points of Japanese propaganda. It has been published in this newspaper on April 30th. The original letter has been translated into English and formally submitted to the League of Nations Investigation Team. Also, the English version of "The Reign of Terror in Shanghai for a Month," a direct record from the Shanghai Western press about Japanese atrocities, has been published. The French version of the Chamber of Commerce's letter is also being printed. The method for reprinting is as follows: those who wish to reprint can contact the China Weekly Review office at 19 Museum Road in this city. The reprinting methods are as follows: (1) Type A: the Chamber of Commerce's letter and lengthy article are printed in English and French. The English version has been published, and the French version is being printed. Type B: "The Reign of Terror in Shanghai" is exclusively in English and has also been published. Since not many copies of the above two types have been printed, and it is difficult to distribute them widely to various countries, it is hoped that individuals and organizations at home and abroad will reprint them as much as possible and disseminate them widely. (2) The reprinting cost is approximately thirty yuan per thousand copies. If more copies are reprinted at the same time, the cost can be reduced. The remaining funds can be refunded or used to print additional copies, as desired. (3) Overseas postage is five cents per copy, or fifty yuan per thousand copies. (4) To avoid duplication when mailing overseas, please submit the mailing list to the contact office for verification (the list must specify the recipient's occupation for easy checking). If you wish the contact office to provide the mailing list, the typing fee is five yuan per thousand copies. If you wish the contact office to handle the mailing, the typing and packaging fee is fifteen yuan per thousand copies. If two items are mailed to the same address, it will be counted as one. (5) Postage for reprinting outside of this city will be added separately. (6) The cost of obtaining individual copies, including postage, is five cents each. (7) Overseas local reprinting can save on postage.

Two Cases of Arresting Reactionaries on May Day 114

The day before yesterday was Labor Day, and radical elements took advantage of this opportunity to engage in large-scale propaganda. Therefore, at 9:00 a.m. the day before yesterday, a man named Wan Guohua (also known as Zhang Funian) from Xuzhou, living at 30 Datong Lane, Kunming Road, near Taopeng Road in Yangshupu, was distributing 374 communist leaflets along the way and shouting slogans. He was spotted by Chinese Detective Yang Peisheng and Western Detective De Lubo of the Yangshupu Police Station and was immediately arrested and taken to the police station. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Second Branch of the Higher Court, where Judge Zhao presided over the trial. After the police lawyer Li Zhishan presented the case, the defendant claimed that he was walking here and was mistakenly arrested, and he made various evasive arguments. The court ordered a postponement for further trial.

Dong Manni, a Jiangxi native, was arrested at 1:10 p.m. the day before yesterday at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Simalu, holding reactionary leaflets and shouting reactionary slogans. At the same time, several companions gathered to march. Chinese Detective Cao Qishan of the Laoza Police Station stepped forward to arrest him. Dong confessed that there were more leaflets and books hidden at 76 Avenue Paul Beau and 141 Xinxin Lane on Rue Pere Robert in the French Concession. The police, together with the French Concession Police, went to search and found a large number of reactionary books, etc. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Second Branch of the Higher Court. After the police lawyer Li Zhishan presented the case, Judge Zhao questioned him and ordered a postponement for further trial.

Central Bank Inspection Report 115

No. 123

The 123rd inspection report of the Central Bank's issuance reserve states: This committee, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible notes of this bank. On April 30, 1932, Supervisor Qin Runqing conducted the 123rd inspection at the Issuing Bureau of this bank. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible notes issued: 27,225,024 silver dollars, including 24,453,417 silver dollar notes and 2,692,607 fractional currency notes. Total amount of convertible note reserve: 27,225,024 silver dollars, including 21,645,748 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve is held in the issuing vault of this bank at 18,596,868.45 yuan, in branches in various ports at 1,385,177 yuan, and in other banks at 1,663,702.55 yuan. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 5,579,276 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued: 375,000 customs gold units. Total amount of customs gold convertible note reserve: 375,000 customs gold units, including US$150,000 deposited with banks in this port, calculated at a fixed rate of 0.40 to customs gold. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guaranteed reserve should be 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guaranteed reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. April 30, 1932, Central Bank Supervisory Board.

"Whip" Weekly Publication 116

"Whip" Weekly has recently been published in Beiping and has now reached Volume 1, Issue 8. The content of the publication offers incisive criticisms of current affairs and fair judgments of the party and government, adhering to facts and being impartial in both academic theory and practice. For several years, freedom of speech has been almost completely suppressed, and this freedom has only recently begun to recover gradually. Unfortunately, much of it is empty and clamorous, without contributing to the overall situation. However, judging from the text of each issue of "Whip" Weekly, it is still able to avoid extremism and the prevailing attitude of sensational propaganda. Its criticism of the authorities is strict in wording and justified in reasoning, without losing the integrity of representing public opinion. It is reported that the members of the publication are all faculty members of various universities in Beiping, who share the writing responsibilities. The future development of this publication can be predicted. The general distribution office of the publication is at 27 Lukmicang, Beiping. It is sold in Shanghai by Minzhi Bookstore and Dadong Bookstore, and in Ningbo by Minzhi. The price per issue is four cents, and the annual subscription is two yuan.

Mother-in-law Killed with a Knife, One-Year Imprisonment 123

Bian Yaoqin from Ningbo and his mother-in-law, Mrs. Peng Chen, from Tongzhou, lived together at No. 77 Yangshupu Road. Bian was addicted to prostitution and gambling, spending money like water, which caused Mrs. Peng to borrow hundreds of taels of silver. She inevitably scolded him from time to time. On the 24th of last month, late at night, Bian suddenly became vicious and sneaked into Mrs. Peng's bedroom with a kitchen knife. While she was sound asleep, he slashed at her head. Fortunately, Mrs. Peng covered her head with a quilt at the time, so she did not suffer serious injuries. She woke up screaming for help, and Bian fled. Mrs. Peng reported the incident to the Yangshupu Police Station, who sent detectives to arrest Bian and escort him to the First Special District Court. Bian insisted that he only used the back of the knife to strike slightly to vent his resentment. The case was submitted for sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong presided over the trial at the First Higher Court and sentenced Bian Yaoqin to one year of imprisonment for using methods sufficient to cause serious injury and harming a collateral relative. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the sentence at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

Educational News Headlines

Ministry of Education Specifies Uniform Implementation of Credit System 127

The Ministry of Education has specified a uniform method for implementing the credit system. In addition to ordering direct schools and colleges, it has also issued an order to the education departments of provinces and cities to forward to public and private universities and specialized schools for compliance. The order states: After investigation, the university regulations stipulate that the credit system and the academic year system should be used simultaneously, but the implementation methods of the credit system vary greatly among universities. In order to unify this, the following methods are specifically stipulated: (1) All terms such as (grade points) should be uniformly changed to credits. (2) For subjects requiring after-class self-study, one hour of class per week for a full semester counts as one credit. For subjects that are practical or do not require after-class self-study, two hours count as one credit. (3) The duration of study at the university is generally four years. During the four-year study period, students must successfully complete 112 credits. (4) Students in each department of the university are limited to a maximum of 40 credits and a minimum of 30 credits in the first two years, and a maximum of 36 credits and a minimum of 30 credits in the last two years. (5) The credits mentioned in the above articles refer to general subjects. Party principles, military training, and physical education are not included. The duration of study for medical schools is different, and the credits will be announced separately after further regulations. The above points will be implemented starting from 1932. In addition to separate orders, this order is issued for compliance. This order.

The Ministry of Education Interprets Doubts Regarding the Executive Director of the Education Association 130

The Ministry of Education previously received a request from the Hebei Education Department for an interpretation of the doubts regarding the executive director of the Education Association, and had previously replied by telegram. Now, it has received a request from the Jiangsu Education Department for an explanation of various points, which are largely the same as before. It copied and replied to the Jiangsu Education Department, stating: All executive directors elected in accordance with Article 12 of the Detailed Implementation Rules of the Education Association Law, after being reported to the supervisory authority, unless the executive director has committed one of the circumstances listed in Article 25 of the Education Association Law, should be immediately removed from the position of director, and the vacancy should be filled in accordance with Article 14 of the Detailed Implementation Rules of the Education Association Law, and a new executive director should be elected and reported to the supervisory authority. Otherwise, the originally elected executive director may not be removed and replaced midway due to the dissatisfaction of the majority of directors.

Administrative Plan of the Ministry of Education for April, May, and June 131

Revise and Promulgate Course Standards for Senior, Junior High Schools, Elementary Schools, and Kindergartens

—Formulate Regulations on the Employment and Treatment of Teachers in Universities and Middle Schools—

—Formulate Measures for the Joint Examination of Middle School Graduates—

The Ministry of Education recently submitted the three-month (April to June 1932) administrative plan for the fourth period of 1931 to the Executive Yuan for record. The original text of the plan is as follows:

▲Items Concerning Higher Education

(1) Continue to sort out the first drafts of the university curriculum and equipment standards that have been collected. (2) Formulate regulations on the employment and treatment of university teachers. (3) Formulate regulations on university student enrollment and graduation examinations. (4) Formulate implementation measures for scholarships for students in colleges and universities. (5) Formulate registration measures for overseas students returning to the country. (6) Continue to process the registration of private colleges and universities. (7) Continue to review academic organizations approved for registration by various provinces and cities. (8) Continue to review the entrance qualifications of new students in colleges and universities. (9) Continue to review the grades of college and university graduates. (10) Issue statistics on national higher education from August 1928 to July 1931. (11) Compile statistics on overseas students over the years. (12) Investigate and compile the losses suffered by public and private colleges and universities in Shanghai during the recent invasion by Japanese soldiers.

Items Concerning Secondary Education

(1) Formulate measures for the joint examination of middle school graduates. (2) Formulate various matters that should be given special attention in moral education in middle schools in the future. (3) Compile and print statistics on secondary education for 1929. (4) Convene a committee to design vocational education. (5) Revise and promulgate course standards for senior and junior high schools. (6) Promulgate the investigation of the general situation of education in various provinces and cities. (7) Propose a plan to improve the qualifications and treatment of middle school teachers.

▲Items Concerning Elementary Education

(1) Formulate measures for the joint examination of elementary school graduates. (2) Formulate various matters that should be given special attention in moral education in elementary schools in the future. (3) Revise and promulgate course standards for elementary schools and kindergartens. (4) Formulate and promulgate measures to promote compulsory education in stages and regions. (5) Formulate measures for educational administrative agencies to guide local education. (6) Prepare to compile standards for moral education in elementary schools. (7) Promulgate measures for the examination of elementary school teachers. (8) Promulgate the investigation of the general situation of education in various provinces, regions, counties, and cities.

▲Items Concerning Social Education

(1) Promulgate a list and comparison table of social education expenditures in various provinces and cities in 1931. (2) Organize and compile questionnaires from people's schools and vocational supplementary schools in various provinces and cities, and selectively compile and issue them to various provinces and cities for reference. (3) Continue to organize historical materials on social education administration since the founding of the Republic of China. (4) Compile and print a general overview of national social education in 1929. (5) Investigate the implementation of social education in various provinces and cities. (6) Continue to formulate standards for the establishment of various social education undertakings. (7) Continue to select and compile appropriate books related to national salvation and order public and private libraries across the country to purchase them as much as possible, and guide the public to read them. (8) Formulate a survey form for people's education centers in various provinces and cities, and order the education departments of various provinces and cities to forward them to their subordinates for completion and submission to the Ministry for statistics. (9) Formulate a survey form for libraries in various provinces and cities, and order the education departments of various provinces and cities to forward them to their subordinates for completion and submission to the Ministry for statistics. (10) Propose regulations for the Educational Film Committee. (11) Compile the National Calendar for 1933.

▲Items Concerning Mongolian and Tibetan Education

(1) Order all leagues, banners, and religious leaders to instruct local schools to pay special attention to teaching materials such as national humiliation and national crisis. (2) Continue to order all leagues, banners, and religious leaders to actively promote elementary schools and secondary schools. (3) Continue to investigate the number of school-age children in all leagues and banners. (4) Continue to order the subordinate leagues, banners, and religious leaders to submit educational administrative plans and work reports for 1931 separately for review. (5) Continue to select and translate party principles and various accessible books in Mongolian and Tibetan.

▲Items Concerning Compilation and Translation

(1) Compile the first education yearbook. (2) Compile textbooks for elementary and middle schools. (3) Continue to compile scientific terminology.

▲Items Concerning Review

(1) Continue to review textbooks and teaching books for elementary and middle schools and people's schools. (2) Continue to review children's reading materials. (3) Continue to review educational instruments and specimens. (4) Continue to review books on the history of national humiliation, diplomatic history, and those related to party principles.

Local News

15th Anniversary of the China Vocational Education Society 133

▲Anniversary Ceremony to be Held on the 6th of this Month

The China Vocational Education Society was established in May 1917 and has been working diligently to promote and advocate vocational education in society and to provide suggestions and contributions to the government. Its efforts in vocational education have achieved considerable results. It is reported that in addition to compiling and distributing commemorative publications and soliciting artistic works and educational opinions from comrades, the society will also hold a 15th anniversary ceremony and a foundation-laying ceremony for the school's reconstructed school buildings at the China Vocational School on Yingdong Road, outside Xiaoximen, at 9:00 a.m. on May 6th. All Shanghai members of the society, current staff members, faculty members of affiliated schools, vocational education workers, graduates, staff members of other affiliated institutions, those who have been successfully introduced by the vocational guidance center, and those who participated in the founding conference of the society 15 years ago must participate together to commemorate the occasion. The original letter and methods for soliciting commemorative items are appended below:

Circular: We respectfully inform you that the Republic of China has been established for over twenty years, and our society has been established for fifteen years. The 6th of May this year marks the 15th anniversary. Thinking of the many hardships of the times, we are greatly alarmed by the fleeting time. In the past fifteen years, the colleagues of our society have received assistance from society and have been driven by conscience. Although we have worked diligently, we dare not say that we have accomplished much. However, due to the expansion of our undertakings, we are constantly aware of our lack of ability, so we are often ashamed of excessive praise. On the occasion of the anniversary, in order to encourage interest and improve our work, we plan to ask you, without hesitation, to give us words of wisdom, poetry, and articles, and to express your high opinions on vocational education based on your own views. We will decorate the pages, gather them into rare treasures, and list the articles as a model for future generations. We have prepared the methods and enclosed them with this letter. We respectfully ask for your consideration and wish you well. Thank you for your attention.

▲Methods for Soliciting Artistic Works and Educational Opinions from Members of the Society (1) Our society has been established for fifteen years, during which it has experienced many hardships. It seems worthwhile to give it a proper commemoration. Soliciting poems, calligraphy, and art from members of the society is intended to permanently preserve this beautiful memory, to promote the spirit of national art, and to encourage the interest of the staff, hoping to improve work efficiency. (2) In addition to poems, calligraphy, and paintings, we seek high opinions on vocational education. The viewpoint may be based on our society, the entire nation and society, a part of the city and countryside, the entire nation, a part of the youth, or other areas, such as the system, organization, or method. The length of the text is not limited. If you can offer pointed criticism, the office of our society will earnestly indicate the direction of progress, which would be greatly appreciated by our colleagues. (3) Poems, calligraphy, and paintings may be submitted at your convenience, without any restrictions. It is best to have everything, but it is also good to have only one. If there are other artistic works that cannot be expressed on paper and you are willing to donate them for commemoration, they are also welcome. (4) The paper for poems, calligraphy, and paintings should be one foot and five inches long and one foot wide. The color and material are not restricted. For the expression of opinions, please write on ordinary letter paper. (5) Please send the donated art and opinions to us before May 21st of this year. (6) The purpose of soliciting artistic works is to showcase the art of our comrades and to preserve them permanently as a commemoration of our society. We regret that we cannot offer any remuneration. Thank you for your understanding.

▲Scheduled to Begin This Thursday

In the wake of its successful amateur tournament, the Shanghai Billiards Amateur Association has suddenly launched a very interesting competition, a novelty in Shanghai, namely the Shanghai Marker Professional Championship, which will begin this Thursday.

▲Number of Participants and Motivation Behind the Event. At the time of the international high-level billiards competition, when the association decided to hold the event, thirteen markers from seven famous clubs participated. The seven clubs are: Shanghai Banking Club, Shanghai General Club, Baohua East Club, French Business Club, International Sports Club Club, Portuguese Club, and International Merchant Marine Club.

▲Competition Method. Initially, each game will be 400 points, the final will be 500 points, starting on the 5th and closing on the 13th. The location is in the billiards room of the Linhua General Club at 3 Beijing Road. Two games will be played daily, admission is one yuan.

Moreover, the outcome of this competition is related not only to their personal reputation but also to the glory of the groups they represent. All thirteen markers are preparing to win, and a heated and intense competition can be expected in the coming days.

Gold Standard Continues Strong at 6.7 Taels 136

▲Gold Trading Only Half Day. Yesterday, May 2nd, due to the Spring Race Day, the Gold Exchange, as usual, only operated for the morning session. The gold standard trend was soaring, but the trading volume was only two or three taels at most, and ultimately rose by seven taels or so. The silver market fell slightly the day before, but the industry's will was firm. The market opened high and fluctuated little. The foreign exchange market was good, and banks were unwilling to sell easily, so the market felt even stronger, with a sense of prosperity. All the May public bonds have now expired and have begun to be collected. Run Changyu and others collected about 3,700 bonds, while those who released them were spot dealers, etc. The market situation yesterday is recorded below.

▲Morning Opening Up Three Taels and Three Candareens. From the early morning, the June contract opened up three taels and three candareens, at 733.5 taels. The large bars were 1/16 lower than the small bars. The silver price was the same as before, but private telegrams were 1/8 lower. Bing Xing, Hong Kangyong, and others bought in, followed by 34.5 taels. At 9 o'clock, the British and American announcements showed no prosperity or decline, which was slightly inferior, around 33 taels, which were sold by retail investors. Shortly after, one tael was added, as the American banks absorbed 30.5 yuan for this month. Subsequently, Tong Feng, Heng Yi, Feng Yong, Yuan Kangxiang, and others sold out, and the price fell by more than one tael, to 32.2 taels. Heng Yu, Shunli, Qian Changxiang, and others bought in again, at 9:40, to 35.5 taels. Da Decheng and others sold out, falling back more than two taels, to 33.2 taels at 10 o'clock. After entering, the buying side exceeded the Heng. Yuhe, Da Decheng, Zhi Fengyong, Hong Kangyong, Yi Fengyong, and others all entered, jumping 3.5 taels, to 36.7 taels around 10:30. Zhi Fengyong, Bing Xing, and others took advantage of this to sell, and Zhejiang offered a recent British gold price of 8 pence, and Mitsui offered June American gold at 5625, and July at 625, so the price fell by two taels. Until 11 o'clock, it was 34 taels. Suddenly, Zhi Fengyong, Heng Yu, and others came to buy in, and Shanghai bought July American gold at 625, so it added two taels. At 11:30, it was 36.2 taels. At this time, Tong Taichang and others sold out, and the price immediately fell by a small amount, to 34.3 taels. In a flash, it was rumored that a certain bank had opened up spot trading, and people's hearts were shaken, and buyers became diligent. However, after detailed inquiries, it was actually that the exchange rate was tight, and Qian Changxiang, Yi Fengyong, and others bought in, which led to it. The price rose by three or four taels, and at 11:50, it was 38 taels. The recent American gold only settled at 375, but many zero-lot buyers and scalpers took advantage of this to sell out, so it fell back by one tael, to 36.8 taels. Then it closed at 36.9 taels, which was 6.7 taels higher than last Saturday. However, it continued to rise to eight taels, which was dragged in by Yi Fengyong and others. Yesterday's half-day maximum was 38 taels, and the minimum was 32.2 taels, a difference of 5.8 taels. Red bars increased by 5.25 taels.

▲Transactions with More Buying Than Selling. According to surface transactions, Yuan Mao Yong, Qian Changxiang, Shunli, Futai Heng, Hong Kangyong, and Bing Xing all bought in. Zhi Fengyong, Da Decheng, Yuan Tai, Yuhe, Heng Yu, and others had frequent buying and selling. Yi Fengyong, Yuan Kangxiang, and others sold out and then bought in. Most of the other firms bought more than they sold.

Tightly Traded Exchange Market 137

Active Trading by Chinese Merchants

British American Tobacco Company Settling Accounts

Yesterday, Monday, overseas silver markets typically have no telegrams, but the previous telegram reported that the British silver fell slightly, and the American silver did not change. The exchange rate also did not change. The HSBC list did not change, but the internal market seemed good. It initially appeared strong, then flat, and became tighter at noon. As a result, the British and American exchange rates each decreased by 125 compared to last Saturday, so the gold price trend was sharp. Chinese merchants were very active in trading, and hedgers bought in. The British gold was only 20,000 to 30,000 pounds, and the American gold was 300,000 to 400,000 yuan, mostly for settlement. It was also heard that the British American Tobacco Company was also settling accounts. It was said that the afternoon was a holiday due to the first day of the Western merchants' spring race.

Turnaround in the Silver Market 139

Price of Interest Suddenly Rises by Four Li

Silver Borrowing Becomes Loose and Excessive

▲Market Overview. In the past two days, because the money industry cancelled the interbank remittance of various Chinese and foreign payments, free flow has been achieved, and the situation has suddenly become lively. Various bills, both Chinese and foreign, can now circulate freely without the need for reserves. With the turnaround in the market, the price of interest has become prosperous and suddenly increased. Silver borrowing has become loose and excessive, which is also the first good phenomenon since the January 28th Incident.

▲Interest Rate and Borrowing Price. (Silver Interest) In the early market, some people also bought the interest rate, which made it quite colorful. The closing price was 1.25 li higher than the early market the day before, at 7 qian and 0.2 li. At noon, it suddenly continued to rise by 3 li, to 7 qian and 0.45 li. The total increase between the two markets was 4 li and strong, and people's hearts became energetic again. (Silver Borrowing) In the early market, transfer and silver borrowing only opened at 5 fen, which was 4 fen lower than the previous morning. In the noon market, it actually borrowed for free, which was the first sound since the war. Banks had no list to list, and there was no way to add water to the transfer. As a result, the market was all borrowed and transferred for free.

▲Subsidiary Coin Market. In the morning, Jiangnan small silver dollars were also slightly bought, and the price was 1 li higher, at 6 qian, 1 fen, and 1 li, with a transaction of 7,500 jiao. At noon, someone released a large amount, and the result was a sharp drop of 6 li, only counting 6 qian and 0.5 li, with a transaction of 4,000 jiao. Guangdong small silver dollars also rose with the silver interest rate. The early market was 6 qian and 0.2 li, and the noon market was 6 qian and 0.3 li, with transactions of 105,000 jiao in the early market and 35,000 jiao in the noon market. Steel dollars increased by 1,000 wen, to 420,500 wen.

▲Silver Dollar Inflow and Outflow. (Silver Funds) Due to the spring races, the Bund was closed in the afternoon, but the banks' receipt of payments was still not weak. Chinese banks received 2.67 million to 2.7 million in payments, foreign banks received 1.7 million to 1.8 million in payments, 1 million in advances, over 600,000 in customs duties, over 600,000 in foreign funds, 1.45 million to 1.5 million in foreign exchange payments, 70,000 to 80,000 in discounted remittances, 1.3 million to 1.4 million in goods payments, 1.5 million in special payments, over 2 million in settlements, 400,000 in memberships, 500,000 in warehouse outflows, over 34 million in money shop silver public bonds, over 3.7 million in silver transfer payments from money shops, and no news of remittances from various routes. (Foreign Funds) 350,000 was made in the early market for foreign exchange payments and 525,000 in the noon market. 65,000 banknotes in the early market and 70,000 in the noon market. Banks traded 300,000 in the early market and 500,000 in the noon market. The inflow and outflow of foreign accounts of various banks was over 1.8 million, and the inflow and outflow of banknotes was over 1 million. Money shops received over 5.3 million in foreign public bonds, and over 2.5 million in foreign transfer payments. Over 1.8 million in foreign loans were borrowed, and small money shops traded over 600,000. The details of the coming and going were not detailed.

A Glimpse of the Good Scenery After the Recovery 140

Various Industries Seem to Have the Possibility of Activity

Money Industry Cancels Interbank Remittances

Since the Shanghai Incident, it was impossible to talk about the rise and fall of commerce. Now there is hope for peace, and various commercial activities are gradually returning to their original state, especially the cancellation of interbank remittances by the money industry, which is most welcomed by various industries. As a result, business has greatly progressed and is quite prosperous. Here is a brief record of what I have heard, for the reader's information.

(1) The Exchange began to trade with each other, and the prices of various bonds rose sharply, and two or three bonds were actually suspended due to excessive prices. (2) Wholesale merchants are issuing tickets for goods one after another, and Chinese and foreign goods can still be exchanged for money shop tickets, which are actively circulated, as in the past. (3) Telegrams and letters for foreign remittances and purchases are pouring in, and purchases from the Nanyang Islands are particularly strong. (4) Various ports purchase goods, such as summer and new autumn necessities, regardless of food or supplies, and they are all bought with courage. (5) It is heard that cotton yarn is being shipped to Guangdong, Hubei, Anhui, Shandong, Chongqing, Hunan, and other places, piled up at the docks, and it is also heard that quite a lot is being shipped to other ports. (6) The prosperity of domestic goods wholesale is more successful than before the January 28th Incident, because at that time it was the end of the year and there was not much demand. Now is the time for each good to expand its sales, so the situation is particularly courageous. (7) The financial industry's silver supply and the purchase of goods are quite active, and a lot of money is received. Although yesterday was the afternoon closing of the horse races, the prosperity was still undiminished, which shows that there will be good news for us when the races are open all day for three days.

Zhejiang Province Plans Silkworm Cocoon Cooperation 147

Borrowing 1.8 Million Yuan... Establishing a Cooperative Sales Committee. The Morning People of Each Department in Zhejiang Province, in View of the Fact That Last Year's Spring Silkworms Suffered Heavily from the Damage of the Weather, and Furthermore, the National Disaster Was in Full Swing, the Rural Economy Declined, and the Amount of Spring Silkworm Rearing Was Greatly Reduced. Statistics Only Reached 30-40% of Previous Years, but the Silk and Silk Industries Both Failed, and the Finance Was Extremely Tight. There Was No Ability to Collect Cocoons, and No One Asked About the Cocoon Shops in Each Department. In the Future, Cocoon Households Would Definitely Not Be Able to Benefit. Both the Financial and Construction Halls Had This in Mind. Now, They Are Establishing a Silkworm Cocoon Relief Association With the Silver Money Industry, and Decided to Borrow 1.8 Million Yuan to Plan the Silkworm Cocoon Cooperative Transportation and Sales Committee. The Financial and Construction Halls Together Sent Three Committee Members, the Silver Group Sent Three People, and Another Three Experts Were Extended to Be Committee Members. The Cocoon Production Counties in the Entire Province Were Divided Into Several Regions, and Several Cooperative Societies Were Established to Lend and Pay the Farm Silkworms Appropriate Funds and Sell Cocoons on Behalf of the Cocoon Households as Their Business. It Is Heard That the Previous Loan Has Been Negotiated With the Silver Group and Is Expected to Be Realized in the Near Future.

A Bundle of Wuyuan Tea News 148

▲The Head Tea Develops Prosperously. Although the Winter Climate Was Very Cold in Wuyi Spring Tea, the Tea Trees Facing the Wind on the Plains Were Fortunately Not Injured. This Spring, the Weather Was Clear and the Rain Was Evenly Distributed. The Tea Trees Facing the Sun Had Already Shown Sparrow Beaks After Qingming. The Weather Suddenly Turned Warm and Rainy These Days, and the Tea Leaves Drew More Buds. According to Mountain Households, the Tea Body Development This Year Is More Prosperous Than in the Past, and the Output Will Definitely Be a Good Harvest. If the Weather Continues to Be Clear and Warm and Not Cold, the Head Tea Can Be Opened in Ten Days. However, the Budding of Mountain Tea Is Slower Due to the Shelter of Trees and Soil.

▲Mao Feng Can Be Released Soon. Mao Feng, Made in the Yibei Yanchuan, Zhangcun, and Jinzhu Areas, Has Always Been Famous. The Fragrant and Pure Quality and Taste Are Not Inferior to Hangzhou's Longjing and Fujian's Wuyi. In Recent Years, It Has Become a Valuable Item Because of the Increasing Number of Distant Purchasers and Self-Addiction to Gifts. Recently, Mountain Households Intend to Collect and Make It in Time Because the Tea Buds Are Budding Green and Tender. It Is Heard That This Year's Tea Households Are Even More Actively Making Improvements to the Mao Feng Making Method in Order to Become Treasures. If the Weather Is Clear and Bright, There Can Be New Releases Within Days.

▲The Lack of Foreign Impact on Tea Funds. The Tea Foreign Funds of Each Firm in This County, in Addition to the Supply of Local Merchants, Have Always Relied on Jingde, Raozhou, Leping, Tunxi, and Other Ports as a Large Source. This Year, the County Seat and Townships of This County Have Very Little Current Foreign Income and Very Thin Foreign Stock Due to the Impact of the Situation and the Sluggish Commerce. Although Tun Jing Le Has Abundant Current Foreign and the Foreign Li Is Low, They Are Deeply Concerned About the Dangers of Transporting Current Far Away in View of the Fact That the Bandit Atmosphere Is Not Peaceful, So Each Firm Has Been Sparing No Effort in Searching for the Current Foreign of Merchants Recently. Because Merchants Have Extensive Foreign Use and the Supply Does Not Meet the Demand, They Have All Suppressed the Ticket Price, Selling Only More Than 1,360 Yuan per Thousand Taels, Which Is 20-30 Yuan Less Than Rao Le and Other Places. It Is Expected That When the New Tea Is Listed, It Will Definitely Feel the Pain of Foreign Shortage.
