Martyr Zhu 150

— Jing

Martyr Zhu Zhuoting was from Qiantang. He studied at Fudan University in Shanghai. When the Shanghai Incident suddenly arose, he happened to be in the Xinmin Dormitory on North Sichuan Road, which led to his capture by the violent Japanese. At that time, the Japanese army's plan of aggression could not succeed, so they shifted their poison to good people and treated them cruelly. The pen could not bear to describe it. Students were even worse. Fourteen prisoners in the same dormitory were imprisoned in one room. They were forced to confess who had the military uniforms in the dormitory. Otherwise, they would all be subjected to extreme torture. The martyr could not bear to see the fourteen people die together, so he stood up and responded. He scolded the Japanese slaves and confessed that he was a member of the Fudan Volunteer Army and had nothing to do with the others. The martyr then died, and the others in the same difficulty escaped. In the past, the martyr had a strong personality and served in the school's volunteer army. He was able to do his duty. His love for the country was deeply rooted. Therefore, his death this time was to repay his long-cherished wish. The martyr had only been away from Hangzhou for two days when he suffered this misfortune. He died at the age of twenty-six.

The Jinan Incident and the Shanghai Incident 151

— Wang Junfang

May 3rd, 1928. Japanese soldiers marched into Jinan Prefecture, Shandong Province, our China. The cries of our compatriots echoed like ghosts. Even the diplomat Mr. Cai Gongshi died with them. How terrible! After the Japanese soldiers invaded, there were many negotiations. It wasn't until May of the following year that the Japanese soldiers occupying Jinan were willing to withdraw.

At the time of the troop withdrawal, the general public was outraged and heartbroken by the Japanese soldiers' forceful occupation of Jinan and the killing of compatriots the previous year. It seemed that the resentment had subsided a lot. But at that time, I had a different feeling. I dared not be optimistic. Because at that time, the Japanese troop withdrawal was only a temporary return of some of China's jurisdiction over Shandong. They could still come to occupy our territory and kill our compatriots at any time.

"It is terrible for the Japanese soldiers to come and not leave. But is it impossible for them to come again once they have left? Does our country have the power to ensure that Japanese soldiers will not come again? I'm afraid that if they come again, they won't go to Jinan. They will kill Chinese compatriots in another place. If things go wrong, they might even come to Shanghai on the south bank of the Yangtze River to kill people. It can be imagined that the degree of danger to our people is the same whether the Japanese soldiers withdraw or not. Considering the compatriots outside of Jinan, the danger is only increased."

Although I had such wild thoughts as mentioned above at that time, after some time, I gradually forgot them. Oh no. On the evening of January 28th this year, my previous wild thoughts unfortunately became a reality. Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, Baoshan, Zhenru, Nanxiang, Taicang, Dachang, Huangdu…

…Compatriots in areas near Shanghai are now being burned and killed by Japanese soldiers. They are crying like ghosts, displaced, and everything has been reduced to ashes. Isn't it much more severe than the degree of harm inflicted by Japanese soldiers on Jinan compatriots five years ago? Thinking of the past and present, today, in the midst of the chaos in Shanghai, commemorating the May 3rd Jinan Massacre of a few years ago, I truly feel "how heartbreaking it is."

Thinking carefully about the Jinan Incident in the past and the Shanghai Incident now, I cannot help but have a few more words to tell my compatriots. The Japanese soldiers who came before have left, but now they have come again. Those from other countries who have not come (?) can also come. The reason is simple. Because our country can simply be said to have no national defense at present. There is only "provincial defense." "Provincial defense" can only be used to divide up territory and cannot be used to resist foreign enemies. Oh, our poor people. How should we fight against the old and new warlords and imperialists in the future to preserve the vitality of our Chinese nation?

World News in Brief 152

— Haike

Strange Jobs. There are many strange jobs in the city of London. But the strangest of all is watching chimneys. The London City Council has a strict ban on black smoke coming out of factory chimneys. Anyone who violates the ban will be severely punished. Therefore, most factories employ people who specialize in watching chimneys to avoid violations and penalties. In the city of Gilsee, there is a subway power station that has built a small house on the roof for the chimney watcher to live in. He walks in and out from time to time, watching the large chimneys. He holds a small glass screen with four different colors of glass, light and dark. As soon as he sees smoke, he looks at it through the screen and compares it with the color on the glass. If the smoke is the same as the darkest color, he immediately gets busy and presses an electric button. Immediately, the bell rings loudly and the bugles blare. Dangerous signals appear in many offices. Then, the stoker tries to suppress the black smoke. The chimney watcher's responsibility is considered fulfilled.

The Story of Rongma Shuanglou (40) 153

— Seeking Happiness Studio Owner

Chapter 5: Breaking off relations with a thankless person brings unexpected encounters with generous guests. A plan to resolve affection is most difficult to carry out and is not in any way comparable to having beautiful woman's favor. Liang Xiaoyun lowered her face and said, "You underestimate me too much. How can you be so sure that I don't deserve to have a good idea? Well, let me tell you honestly. If I were to boast, this matter is something that only I can do to help you a lot. You have been friends with me all along, so you can be said to have gained something from the relationship. However, I still need to ask my other friend for help. General Supervisor Ye has a most favored Fifth Concubine. She used to be my best friend. If you want to work under General Supervisor Ye, there is no need to take the detour of applying to the military academy. Just let me communicate with her and mention it to the Fifth Concubine. If she recommends you to General Supervisor Ye, you will definitely get a ready-made letter of appointment. The position will definitely be much higher than a company commander. In the future, with this opportunity for advancement, and if you continue to work hard and form a new team, becoming a senior commander will not be difficult. What do you think? The path that I have considered for you should be good." An Yutian pondered and said, "Of course, this path is very good. It's just a pity that it is not very honorable or legitimate. But I am always grateful for your kindness. Nowadays, people of ambition don't have to be selective about the means to achieve their goals, so I won't bother about that so much. But when you go to the Fifth Concubine to recommend me, how should you phrase it? And what kind of relationship should you say we have?" Although Liang Xiaoyun had a plan in mind, she did not expect An Yutian to ask such a silly question himself. For a moment, she did not know how to answer. She just smiled coldly and said, "That will have to depend on you yourself." After saying that, a maid walked in and said that dinner was ready. Liang Xiaoyun instructed to have it served in the bedroom. Immediately, a table of the most delicious home-cooked meals was brought in. An Yutian still had not had a drop of water or grain in his stomach today. And with Liang Xiaoyun's such attentive persuasion, he could not help but eat his fill. After dinner, he paced back and forth in the room, thinking of Liang Xiaoyun's question to him earlier. It was really between understandable and incomprehensible. He couldn't help but ask for clarification. So he said with a shameless face, "When you see the Fifth Concubine, should you say that we are friends or relatives? Would that work?" Liang Xiaoyun sat on the edge of the bed, with a cigarette in her cherry lips, as if she was thinking about something intently. Hearing that An Yutian was still acting so foolish, she said lightly, "You should decide for yourself. Anyway, I have already decided to help you. You don't know my feelings for you. Please sit here for a while. Let's find some entertainment after dinner to pass the time."

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Republic of China, Year 21, May 3rd, Tuesday (No Additional Charge)

Commentary

A Letter from Mr. Fang 154

— Buddha

The other day, I received three letters from Mr. Fang. One was for Mr. Shi Liangcai, one was for the chief editor, and one was for the editor of this publication. Two were registered,

and one was sent by ordinary mail. The address was Fang Dunfu, but the signature inside the letters was "A Member of the Public." The content of the three letters was exactly the same. He disapproved of and attacked this publication on roughly two points:

1. The Mass Literature section does not approve of old-style poetry.

2. Popular science is too far removed from the masses.

As for whether Mr. Fang sent three letters in one day with other intentions, I do not know, nor do I have the energy or time to explore them. However, I admit that the two points Mr. Fang indicated are indeed somewhat inconsistent with the word "masses." However, I must briefly explain the reasons for my editing and the process involved, and discuss them with the general readers and contributors.

At the beginning of the reform of this publication, I originally wanted to make the content of this publication completely populist, using easy-to-understand language. Science would also be practical and related to ordinary applications. This was the original intention of reforming this publication. In fact, the word "science" was already somewhat inappropriate. According to Liang Rengong,

"The analysis and synthesis of experiential facts to derive a general rule that is closest to the truth, in order to deduce similar things, this kind of learning is called 'science.' The materials changed or the machines constructed by applied science can only be called the results of science and cannot be equated with 'science' itself."

Whether Rengong's explanation is appropriate, I do not know, because his explanation of the meaning of the term science is similar to logic. Logic is originally the study of reasoning, the law of all laws, the learning of all learning, and its function is also like this. This question will naturally be discussed by those who are learned and knowledgeable, and I will not care about it for the time being. However, after trying it for a month,

literature takes the form of vernacular poetry (the so-called new poetry) and vernacular prose, and science also takes the form of easier-to-understand and practical content.

However, after careful selection, there are indeed a few articles in the new poems and new texts that are rich in artistic meaning, but they are not often seen. There are also many that casually describe a few sentences without being profound. Moreover, the definition of the two words "literature and art" is even more difficult. If we speak in a broad sense, none of the articles published in this publication has no artistic value. If we speak in a narrow sense, which article has artistic value and which kind of text can be considered to have artistic value is something that even I do not know.

As for science, it is originally a specialized subject that the masses do not come into contact with. Moreover, most of the contributions submitted by contributors are studies of the principles of various substances, and most of them are not very practical. It is very difficult to choose those that conform to the purpose of the word "masses."

To be honest, the editors of this publication are not only laymen to science, but also have a half-baked understanding of the two words "literature and art" and do not understand them at all. I am deeply grateful to all the contributors who help me every day. However, the space in this publication is limited, and since the war, the front line has been shortened even more, so I have not been able to publish as much as possible. This is what I regret, (to be continued)

Science

Machine Guns 157

— Naizheng

Machine guns occupy a very important position in the army's ordnance, because they are easy to carry and fire bullets quickly, and they have great uses in both defense and offense.

Machine guns can be divided into several parts: gun body, gun, loading machine, continuous shooting machine, and tripod. But their uses are different, so there are five kinds of machine guns in modern times. Now I will describe them separately...

(1) Heavy machine guns fire at a speed of 400 to 700 rounds per minute and require three or four people to manage, but the latest American heavy machine guns can be operated by two people. To transport it, it usually requires horses or cars, but some people also carry it. Its firing range (i.e., range) can reach 13,000 feet, and it is most powerful within 10,000 feet. The Japanese army's Type 3 machine gun is of this type. (2) Light machine guns have a firing speed of 500 to 800 rounds per minute and can be operated by two people. The range is about the same as that of heavy machine guns, but it is more powerful within 7,000 feet. It was invented and had good effectiveness in the first year of the European War. Later, it was vigorously promoted and became the main weapon of the infantry. According to the organization of the national army, each regiment has one machine gun company. Its importance can be seen. The lightest light machine gun weighs only 22 pounds, which is about 16.5 pounds in our country, and is very convenient to carry. Therefore, it is used during charges, but the heavy machine guns mentioned above are mostly used for defense.

(3) Handheld machine guns are petite and exquisite, and weigh even less, only about 13 or 14 pounds. One person can operate it. When not in use, it is held on the shoulder like a rifle. The barrel is the shortest of the five types, so the range is also the shortest. But it is light and easy to operate, easy to hit the enemy, and its power is very fierce in normal distances, so the guards of important figures in our military all use handheld machine guns.

(4) Aircraft machine guns are either installed on aircraft or carried on aircraft for downward strafing or mutual aerial combat. The weight and range are the same as light machine guns, but the firing rate is more than 1,300 rounds per minute. There is also a double-barreled one that can fire at the same time, which is even more fierce.

(5) Anti-aircraft machine guns are used to shoot down aircraft. They are mounted on a frame, with the muzzle pointing upwards, and the barrel forming an angle of 45 degrees to 90 degrees (right angle) with the plane. Within this range, it can be raised and lowered arbitrarily and can be rotated. Its barrel is the longest of the five types, so its range is very long, about 15,000 feet, and it can penetrate the body of an aircraft within 10,000 feet. Because it continuously fires 600 rounds per minute, the bullets fly like a string of beads. If an aircraft is hit by it, it must be hit by at least five bullets. As for its attachments, there is also a reflex sight.

The firing power of machine guns is fierce, the rate is very fast, and the bore is tight and long. The friction of the bullets flying out continuously generates a great deal of heat. Therefore, it must be cooled, otherwise the bore will melt and crack. The old-fashioned gun bore had an extra layer of space outside, storing cold water or other liquids, which had to be replaced from time to time, but the heat could make the water boil, and it would dry out in a short time. Therefore, it was very inconvenient if it encountered a sandy field with no water. Therefore, air cooling has been used in recent years to avoid this disadvantage.

East, West, North, South

Nameless Heroes 158

— Baitao

After January 28th, our army fought against the Japanese army and won repeatedly, and on several occasions, they even captured the enemy's headquarters. During this period, there were many heroic stories that were both tearful and inspiring.

When the war broke out, the most fierce fighting took place in Tiantong'an. Because Tiantong'an was close to the enemy's headquarters, our army and the enemy fought hand-to-hand several times, gaining and losing repeatedly! Later, the enemy did not hesitate to attack with all their strength.

At that time, the situation was very critical. Five soldiers in our army jumped out and petitioned the officer, willing to be a suicide squad to defeat the enemy. The officer granted their request. He took pictures of them and taught them to write their wills. Then, each of them hung a large bomb on their chest and carried a box of gasoline on their back. At the order, they desperately rushed towards the enemy's headquarters, followed by only a few soldiers. These five heroic soldiers rushed into the enemy's headquarters, and immediately the bombs exploded, burning their bodies to the bone. The enemy was unprepared and thought that our main force had arrived, so they were frightened out of their wits and dropped their weapons and ran away. So our army won a great victory and turned the crisis into safety.

It is a pity that these five soldiers did not leave behind their names. To this day, we remember the heroes with a mixture of grief and indignation!

A Corner of Society

The Psychology of the Chinese People 159

— Wu

Every day is the same, I am still sleeping in bed when I hear the newspaper sellers calling out. A simple "Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao... Shishi Xinbao... Shibao," from far to near, and then from thick to thin. But in the early morning light of yesterday, in the hazy spring sleep, I heard "a high-pitched cry, which was different"... It simply made me excited.

"Nanny!" I shouted... "Quickly go buy a copy of Shen Bao.

Originally, I could go to the office to read it, but that would be too late.

"Sir! Sixteen copper coins," the nanny said, returning with the newspaper...

"Oh? Why is it so expensive?"

"I don't know, but he said (today it will be sold more expensively, don't let anyone else have it), and ran off immediately..."

"Yes, yes, I understand." Because I was eager to read it, I didn't want to haggle with her.

Sure enough, the newspaper published the news in the most conspicuous place, and it was also vividly described, using all the skills of description.

Really, this is an amazing piece of news worth recording, otherwise how could the newspaper sellers make a big profit? Even I sincerely respected that person!

Later, in the tram to the office, I had the opportunity to listen to the various brilliant discussions of the Chinese people...

"It's a pity there isn't a XX," a gentlemanly middle-aged man said with a sigh. An old woman followed up by saying...

"Amitabha!"

"But we Chinese don't even have half of one; sigh!" You think? This is a small businessman said sadly. However, he immediately suffered the contemptuous cold eyes of a student sitting opposite him, as if to say, "Why don't you try it yourself?" So the businessman had to lower his head and remain silent. Suddenly, a strong young man in short clothes also joined their conversation.

The tram unknowingly reached its destination, so I hurriedly got off the tram, and in the end I didn't hear the young man's conclusion.

Alas!

A Tragic Scene 160

— New Easy

Characters: Two soldiers who speak Chinese, two girls from Jiangbei (each about seven or eight years old). Location: Wusong.

Time: One day in mid-April 1932. Scene opens.

(Two girls from Jiangbei, faces covered in dirt and clothes tattered, are searching for scraps in a field of rubble. The sky is getting dark. Two soldiers walk from a distance and stop.)

Soldier A: Hey.

(The Jiangbei girls are startled, look up abruptly, trembling slightly, without answering.)

Soldier B: What are you doing?

Girl A: What's it to you?

Girl B: (Looks at Girl A) Let's go.

Soldier A: Stop! (Threateningly)

Soldier B: See if you can go!

(The two girls tremble all over, look around hoping to see someone, but are disappointed, there is no one.)

Soldier A: (Smiling, asks Girl A) How old are you?

Girl A: Eight years old.

Soldier B: (Asks Girl B) How old are you?

Girl B: Also... eight... years... old...

(The two soldiers make strange faces at each other, and after speaking, suddenly burst into maniacal laughter.)

Soldier A and B: You come with us.

(It is getting dark.)

Girl A and B: No... no... to our moms...

Soldier A and B: We have copper coins, come on.

Girl A and B: (Pause, shake their heads, cry) We... we want to go home, it's getting dark.

Soldier A: Cry! (Punches Girl A) Don't cry!

Girl A and B: (Immediately stop crying, but it's dark, walk outwards.)

Soldier A and B: Don't go! (The two grab the two girls and drag them into the broken wall.) We're going to use you two little slaves of a fallen country. You dare to go!

(It is completely dark, nothing can be seen.)

(A girl sobs uncontrollably, her cries stifled by a hand.)

(Muffled cries emerge from the darkness, after some time, the cries cease. There is a burst of maniacal laughter. Then the sound of two people wearing leather shoes walking away. Darkness) Scene closes.

Lamentable Sacrifice for the Enemy 161

— Flood

Next door to my house is a Japanese-owned Ashino Barber Shop; the storefront is decorated very elaborately, so you can always hear the glass spring door "chirping and gurgling"! There is a busy atmosphere. As far as I know, there is a Korean barber named Kim Ding San employed by the shopkeeper; in addition to his formal work, he really seems like a "capable person who does more work" and also has to take on extra tasks… "Buying things, welcoming and seeing off customers."

Every morning, Kim Ding San routinely goes to the Hongkou vegetable market to buy vegetables, and the snow-white dog raised by the shop owner also routinely follows him step by step to visit the vegetable market. Every time he walks in front of my house, if he sees my little brother, he never misses the opportunity to play with him. He often says, "Little baby, how cute!" But for some reason, he doesn't like the little Easterners very much. Sometimes I see him holding the little Easterners publicly, but he always shows some expression of being forced to obey orders.

Unfortunately, like a bolt from the blue, the ruthless artillery fire in Zhabei echoed loudly, turning the residents along Zhaofeng Road into a bleak and fearful tragedy. The boss of the Ashino Barber Shop was very wary of the Chinese people's unanimous anti-Japanese sentiment. In addition to guarding the large glass display windows with iron grilles and wooden boards, he also hid himself deep inside and never dared to show his face easily. But the boss's self-satisfied laughter, "The Great Japanese Empire is promoting its national prestige," often accompanied the rumbling of guns and cannons, constantly being sent over to my house through the cracks in the walls!

Later, as the war became tight, Japanese residents—especially Koreans and Taiwanese—were mostly sent to serve as plainclothes detectives. Kim Ding San, who has always taken "absolute obedience" as his duty, naturally had to go to the trouble of doing this noble deed that he himself was unwilling to do on behalf of the shop owner—being a member of the plainclothes team! When he walked out of the store with his head down, dejected, and was about to report to the XX Headquarters, only the "snow-white" dog, unaware of the times, still stumbled out to chase him, but was finally discovered by the shop owner's wife, who quickly ran over and carried it back.

The bleak and gloomy moon, the sparse and swaying starlight, the patches of war clouds, and the shouts of "kill" by the battlefield warriors, all rushed together; the gunshots and artillery shells created a sky full of red fireflies, and gusts of yin wind brought the cries of the wounded in pain! At dawn one day, at the end of a bridge shrouded in heavy fog, there was a person dressed like a refugee vaguely watching and dodging; unexpectedly, at the other end of the bridge, which was marked by a blue and white flag fluttering in the wind, a few energetic soldiers suddenly stood up, aimed at him in unison, and shouted loudly, "Who is it?" That person was probably "new to the battlefield"! He panicked for a moment and turned around to run, only to hear a "bang" and the person fell down in response. These soldiers rushed to him one after another, only to see him struggling and rolling in a pool of blood, while stammering in a very rusty Shanghai dialect… "This… one… thing… I… feel… that… our… life… is… not… even… as… good… as… a… snow-white… dog… my… enemy… is… still… my… enemy…" Finally, he sighed out an "XX" and became motionless.

The Lower Part of the Film "Fantastic Beasts" is Released in Paris 162

The Paris Theater is releasing the lower part of "Fantastic Beasts" today. The upper part of this film has already received enthusiastic praise from all walks of life. The plot of the lower part is even more intense, and all the strange beasts of the mountains and forests, those not seen in the upper part, all appear in the lower part. There is a scene that writes of the protagonist, Greto's bravery. There are lions and tigers in front, and chasing soldiers in the rear. Greto then climbed up a tree, while poisonous snakes and crocodiles in the water all opened their mouths to wait. Viewers at this point cannot help but squeeze a handful of sweat. However, this film must be transported to other ports to be shown in Shanghai, and the days are few. Those who want to see the real wild beast giant film should not miss the opportunity.

▲ Golden stone artist Zou Mengchan publishes seals. Golden stone scholar and editor of Zhonghua Book Company Zou Mengchan has been immersed in the study of golden stone characters for more than ten years, and his seal carving is especially exquisite. He has both the strength of Ding and Zhao Bei'an's charm, and the roundness and tightness of Wu Changshuo. Recently, he has been devoted to the study of oracle bone inscriptions, and occasionally uses turtle patterns in his seals, which are simple, ancient, and elegant, truly a unique path in seal studies. Because of the increasing number of seekers, he has now set the rules for the price of commissions (send a letter to request them) to make more friends through ink. The address for receiving letters is the second floor of the main store of Zhonghua Book Company on Fourth Malu, and the correspondence address is the editorial office of Zhonghua Book Company.

▲ Civil Judgment: Bai Jinsheng's case against Jiang Zhiliang and others for borrowing money (Main Text) Defendant Jiang Zhiliang shall repay the plaintiff nine hundred and fifty foreign dollars. If he is unable to repay six hundred dollars, the second oldest shall be responsible for repaying it on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne by Jiang Zhiliang.

▲ Xu Sanyuan and others' appeal against the execution objection of Zhou Guisong (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of this instance shall be borne equally by the appellants.

▲ Jin Mengyuan and others' appeal against Wang Renshan and others for debt (Main Text) The appeal is dismissed. The litigation costs of this instance shall be borne equally by each of the appellants.

▲ Civil Instructions: Bian Zuoyi's request for execution. The request is noted. As the case is not yet final, the request will be postponed for discussion in this instruction.

▲ Mao Kangji's request for assistance in arrest. The request is noted. Please wait for the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court to be entrusted, and the petitioner can go to direct the arrest in this instruction.

▲ Xie Taofu's request for the issuance of a transfer certificate. The request is noted. A letter has been sent to the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau urging them to quickly assess the price so that it can be auctioned according to law. The request to issue a transfer certificate will be postponed for discussion in this instruction.

▲ Zhou Shui's continued request for execution. The request is noted. Please wait for further delivery and inquiry in this instruction.

▲ Shen Peiren's request for execution. The request is noted. Please wait for orders for delivery and inquiry in this instruction.

▲ Sun Genyuan's request for execution. The request is noted. Wait for further delivery and inquiry in this instruction.
